### Round 16: Italian Grand Prix
*Date: 2022-09-11*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 22: Abu Dhabi Grand Prix
*Date: 2022-11-20*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |
